<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>

<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>
<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>
<s> i knew one who had lifted it he sought for his lost heart was tender things to love but found them not alas <\s>
<s> nor was there aught the world contains the which he could approve <\s>
<s> 10 through the unheeding many he did move a splendour among shadows a bright blot upon this gloomy scene a spirit that strove for truth and like the preacher found it not <\s>

<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>
<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>
<s> i knew one who had lifted it he sought for his lost heart was tender things to love but found them not alas <\s>
<s> nor was there aught the world contains the which he could approve <\s>
<s> 10 through the unheeding many he did move a splendour among shadows a bright blot upon this gloomy scene a spirit that strove for truth and like the preacher found it not <\s>

<s> note 4 find cj <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>
<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>
<s> i knew one who had lifted it he sought for his lost heart was tender things to love but found them not alas <\s>
<s> nor was there aught the world contains the which he could approve <\s>
<s> 10 through the unheeding many he did move a splendour among shadows a bright blot upon this gloomy scene a spirit that strove for truth and like the preacher found it not <\s>

<s> note 4 find cj <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>
<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>
<s> i knew one who had lifted it he sought for his lost heart was tender things to love but found them not alas <\s>
<s> nor was there aught the world contains the which he could approve <\s>
<s> 10 through the unheeding many he did move a splendour among shadows a bright blot upon this gloomy scene a spirit that strove for truth and like the preacher found it not <\s>

<s> fragment my head is wild with weeping <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 my head is wild with weeping for a grief which is the shadow of a gentle mind <\s>

<s> note 4 find cj <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>
<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>
<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>
<s> i knew one who had lifted it he sought for his lost heart was tender things to love but found them not alas <\s>
<s> nor was there aught the world contains the which he could approve <\s>
<s> 10 through the unheeding many he did move a splendour among shadows a bright blot upon this gloomy scene a spirit that strove for truth and like the preacher found it not <\s>
<s> notes 6 their ... drear 1839 the shadows which the world calls substance there 1824 <\s>
<s> 7 who had lifted 1839 who lifted 1824 <\s>
<s> garnett relics of shelley 1862 o mighty mind in whose deep stream this age shakes like a reed in the unheeding storm why dost thou curb not thine own sacred rage <\s>

<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>
<s> i knew one who had lifted it he sought for his lost heart was tender things to love but found them not alas <\s>
<s> nor was there aught the world contains the which he could approve <\s>
<s> 10 through the unheeding many he did move a splendour among shadows a bright blot upon this gloomy scene a spirit that strove for truth and like the preacher found it not <\s>
<s> notes 6 their ... drear 1839 the shadows which the world calls substance there 1824 <\s>
<s> 7 who had lifted 1839 who lifted 1824 <\s>
<s> garnett relics of shelley 1862 o mighty mind in whose deep stream this age shakes like a reed in the unheeding storm why dost thou curb not thine own sacred rage <\s>
<s> fragment apostrophe to silence <\s>
<s> garnett relics of shelley 1862 <\s>
<s> a transcript by mrs <\s>
<s> shelley given to charles cowden clarke presents one or two variants silence <\s>
<s> oh well are death and sleep and thou three brethren named the guardians gloomy winged of one abyss where life and truth and joy are swallowed up yet spare me spirit pity me until the sounds i hear become my soul 5 and it has left these faint and weary limbs to track along the lapses of the air this wandering melody until it rests among lone mountains in some ... <\s>
<s> notes 4 spirit 1862 o spirit c c c <\s>
<s> 8 this wandering melody 1862 these wandering melodies ... <\s>
<s> fragment the lake's margin <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 the fierce beasts of the woods and wildernesses track not the steps of him who drinks of it for the light breezes which for ever fleet around its margin heap the sand thereon <\s>
<s> fragment my head is wild with weeping <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 my head is wild with weeping for a grief which is the shadow of a gentle mind <\s>
<s> i walk into the air but no relief to seek or haply if i sought to find it came unsought ); to wonder that a chief 5 among men's spirits should be cold and blind <\s>

<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>

<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>
<s> i knew one who had lifted it he sought for his lost heart was tender things to love but found them not alas <\s>
<s> nor was there aught the world contains the which he could approve <\s>

<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>
<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>
<s> i knew one who had lifted it he sought for his lost heart was tender things to love but found them not alas <\s>
<s> nor was there aught the world contains the which he could approve <\s>
<s> 10 through the unheeding many he did move a splendour among shadows a bright blot upon this gloomy scene a spirit that strove for truth and like the preacher found it not <\s>

<s> note 4 find cj <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>
<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>
<s> i knew one who had lifted it he sought for his lost heart was tender things to love but found them not alas <\s>
<s> nor was there aught the world contains the which he could approve <\s>
<s> 10 through the unheeding many he did move a splendour among shadows a bright blot upon this gloomy scene a spirit that strove for truth and like the preacher found it not <\s>

<s> note 4 find cj <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>
<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>
<s> i knew one who had lifted it he sought for his lost heart was tender things to love but found them not alas <\s>
<s> nor was there aught the world contains the which he could approve <\s>
<s> 10 through the unheeding many he did move a splendour among shadows a bright blot upon this gloomy scene a spirit that strove for truth and like the preacher found it not <\s>

<s> fragment my head is wild with weeping <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 my head is wild with weeping for a grief which is the shadow of a gentle mind <\s>
<s> i walk into the air but no relief to seek or haply if i sought to find it came unsought ); to wonder that a chief 5 among men's spirits should be cold and blind <\s>
<s> note 4 find cj <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>
<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> note 4 find cj <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>
<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> fragment my head is wild with weeping <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 my head is wild with weeping for a grief which is the shadow of a gentle mind <\s>
<s> i walk into the air but no relief to seek or haply if i sought to find it came unsought ); to wonder that a chief 5 among men's spirits should be cold and blind <\s>
<s> note 4 find cj <\s>
<s> published by w m <\s>
<s> rossetti 1870 flourishing vine whose kindling clusters glow beneath the autumnal sun none taste of thee for thou dost shroud a ruin and below the rotting bones of dead antiquity <\s>
<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>
<s> the sight of the works of art was full enjoyment and wonder <\s>
<s> he had not studied pictures or statues before he now did so with the eye of taste that referred not to the rules of schools but to those of nature and truth <\s>
<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>
<s> i knew one who had lifted it he sought for his lost heart was tender things to love but found them not alas <\s>
<s> nor was there aught the world contains the which he could approve <\s>
<s> 10 through the unheeding many he did move a splendour among shadows a bright blot upon this gloomy scene a spirit that strove for truth and like the preacher found it not <\s>
<s> notes 6 their ... drear 1839 the shadows which the world calls substance there 1824 <\s>
<s> 7 who had lifted 1839 who lifted 1824 <\s>
<s> garnett relics of shelley 1862 o mighty mind in whose deep stream this age shakes like a reed in the unheeding storm why dost thou curb not thine own sacred rage <\s>
<s> fragment apostrophe to silence <\s>
<s> garnett relics of shelley 1862 <\s>
<s> a transcript by mrs <\s>
<s> shelley given to charles cowden clarke presents one or two variants silence <\s>
<s> oh well are death and sleep and thou three brethren named the guardians gloomy winged of one abyss where life and truth and joy are swallowed up yet spare me spirit pity me until the sounds i hear become my soul 5 and it has left these faint and weary limbs to track along the lapses of the air this wandering melody until it rests among lone mountains in some ... <\s>
<s> notes 4 spirit 1862 o spirit c c c <\s>
<s> 8 this wandering melody 1862 these wandering melodies ... <\s>

<s> the first entrance to rome opened to him a scene of remains of antique grandeur that far surpassed his expectations and the unspeakable beauty of naples and its environs added to the impression he received of the transcendent and glorious beauty of italy <\s>
<s> our winter was spent at naples <\s>
<s> an outlawed murderer had lived seven days there the pursuit was hot when he was cold <\s>
<s> the birds that were his grave fell dead after their feast in vado's wave <\s>
<s> there must have burned within marenghi's breast 100 that fire more warm and bright than life and hope which to the martyr makes his dungeon ... <\s>
<s> more joyous than free heaven's majestic cope to his oppressor warring with decay or he could ne'er have lived years day by day <\s>
<s> nor was his state so lone as you might think <\s>
<s> he had tamed every newt and snake and toad and every seagull which sailed down to drink those freshes ere the death mist went abroad <\s>
<s> and each one with peculiar talk and play 110 wiled not untaught his silent time away <\s>
<s> and the marsh meteors like tame beasts at night came licking with blue tongues his veined feet and he would watch them as like spirits bright in many entangled figures quaint and sweet 115 to some enchanted music they would dance until they vanished at the first moon glance <\s>
<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> note on poems of 1818 by mrs <\s>
<s> we often hear of persons disappointed by a first visit to italy <\s>
<s> this was not shelley's case <\s>
<s> the aspect of its nature its sunny sky its majestic storms of the luxuriant vegetation of the country and the noble marble built cities enchanted him <\s>

<s> he mocked the stars by grouping on each weed the summer dew globes in the golden dawn and ere the hoar frost languished he could read 120 its pictured path as on bare spots of lawn its delicate brief touch in silver weaves the likeness of the wood's remembered leaves <\s>
<s> and many a fresh spring morn would he awaken while yet the unrisen sun made glow like iron 125 quivering in crimson fire the peaks unshaken of mountains and blue isles which did environ with air clad crags that plain of land and sea and feel ... <\s>
<s> and in the moonless nights when the dun ocean 130 heaved underneath wide heaven star impearled starting from dreams ... <\s>
<s> communed with the immeasurable world and felt his life beyond his limbs dilated till his mind grew like that it contemplated <\s>
<s> his food was the wild fig and strawberry the milky pine nuts which the autumn blast shakes into the tall grass or such small fry as from the sea by winter storms are cast and the coarse bulbs of iris flowers he found 140 knotted in clumps under the spongy ground <\s>
<s> and so were kindled powers and thoughts which made his solitude less dark <\s>
<s> when memory came for years gone by leave each a deepening shade his spirit basked in its internal flame 145 as when the black storm hurries round at night the fisher basks beside his red firelight <\s>
<s> yet human hopes and cares and faiths and errors like billows unawakened by the wind slept in marenghi still but that all terrors 150 weakness and doubt had withered in his mind <\s>
<s> and when he saw beneath the sunset's planet a black ship walk over the crimson ocean its pennon streaming on the blasts that fan it 155 its sails and ropes all tense and without motion like the dark ghost of the unburied even striding athwart the orange coloured heaven 28 <\s>
<s> the thought of his own kind who made the soul which sped that winged shape through night and day 160 the thought of his own country ... <\s>

<s> shelley posthumous poems 1824 <\s>
<s> our text is that of the poetical works 1839 lift not the painted veil which those who live call life though unreal shapes be pictured there and it but mimic all we would believe with colours idly spread behind lurk fear and hope twin destinies who ever weave 5 their shadows o'er the chasm sightless and drear <\s>
<s> i knew one who had lifted it he sought for his lost heart was tender things to love but found them not alas <\s>
<s> nor was there aught the world contains the which he could approve <\s>
<s> 10 through the unheeding many he did move a splendour among shadows a bright blot upon this gloomy scene a spirit that strove for truth and like the preacher found it not <\s>
